<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Item 2.02&nbsp;Results of Operations and Financial Condition.</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On January&nbsp;23, 2008, the Registrant issued a press release and
held a conference call with analysts to report on the results of operations for
the fourth quarter of fiscal year 2007, which ended on November&nbsp;30, 2007.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Furnished with this Form&nbsp;8-K as Exhibit&nbsp;99.1 is a copy of the
press release labeled &#147;McCormick Exceeds Goals for Sales and Profit Growth in
2007; Provides Outlook for 2008,&#148; which includes a Consolidated Income
Statement for the three and twelve month periods ended November&nbsp;30, 2007
and November&nbsp;30, 2006, a Consolidated Balance Sheet of the Registrant as
of November&nbsp;30, 2007 and November&nbsp;30, 2006, and an Consolidated
Statement of Cash Flows for the twelve months ended November&nbsp;30, 2007 and November&nbsp;30,
2006.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Item 9.01 Financial
Statements and Exhibits.</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)&nbsp; Exhibits.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The exhibit to this report is listed in Item 2.02 above and in the Exhibit&nbsp;Index
that follows the signature line.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<body lang="EN-US">

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit 99.1</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><img width="604" height="93" src="g34841mmi001.jpg"></font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">McCORMICK EXCEEDS GOALS FOR SALES AND
PROFIT GROWTH IN 2007; PROVIDES OUTLOOK FOR 2008</font></u></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b>Increased</b><b> sales 7% during 2007. Sales for both the consumer and industrial
business rose 7%.</b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b>Reported earnings per share of $1.73.&#160;
On a comparable basis, excluding restructuring charges, earnings per
share increased 12% to $1.92.</b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b>For</b><b> fiscal year
2008, expect to grow sales 4 to 6% and increase earnings per share 8 to 10% on
a comparable basis.</b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">SPARKS, MD, JANUARY 23 -
- - - McCormick&nbsp;&amp; Company, Incorporated (NYSE:MKC), today reported
results for the fourth quarter and fiscal year ended November&nbsp;30,
2007.&#160; For fiscal year 2007, earnings per
share were $1.73 compared to $1.50 in 2006.&#160;
On a comparable basis, excluding restructuring activities, the Company
increased earnings per share 12% to $1.92 in 2007, compared to earnings per
share of $1.72 in 2006.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Alan D. Wilson, President
and CEO, commented, &#147;We exceeded our goals for sales and profit growth in 2007
with strong contributions from both the consumer and industrial
businesses.&#160; Sales growth of 7% exceeded
our 4 to 6% objective for 2007 with the benefit of favorable foreign exchange
rates and higher pricing.&#160; Success with
new products, revitalization efforts, marketing programs and our acquisition strategy
drove an additional portion of the increase.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;During 2007 we made
great progress with our restructuring program.&#160;
Since the program began we have realized $45 million in annual savings
and are on-track to reach up to $55 million by the end of the program in
2008.&#160; This is an outstanding achievement
which is ahead of our original $50 million goal, and a reflection of the
planning, focus and effort of employees throughout McCormick.&#160; In 2007, these significant cost reductions as
well as pricing actions partially offset steep increases in the cost of several
raw materials including pepper, wheat, soy oil and cheese.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;We increased earnings
per share 12% from 2006 on a comparable basis, well ahead of our initial 8 to
10% goal for 2007.&#160; Sales growth, cost
reductions, improved performance by our joint ventures and lower shares
outstanding each contributed to an outstanding increase in our profits.&#160; In November&nbsp;we announced a 10% increase
in the quarterly dividend per share.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Fiscal year results</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the fiscal year, the
Company increased sales 7% from 2006.&#160; In
local currency the increase was 4%.&#160;
Pricing actions to offset higher material costs and favorable product
mix</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\c900132\08-3484-1\task2631690\3484-1-mm.htm',USER='c900132',CD='Jan 23 16:29 2008' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">drove</font>
much of the increase.&#160; Sales volumes in
international markets were particularly strong with a double-digit increase of
industrial business sales in both Europe and the Asia/Pacific region.&#160; In the U.S., higher sales volume in the
consumer business was driven by incremental sales from the Simply Asia Foods
business acquired in June&nbsp;of 2006, and strong growth of Hispanic items,
gourmet products and grinders, offset in part by reduced sales to warehouse
clubs.&#160; While the U.S. industrial
business achieved increased sales to food manufacturers, sales to food service
customers declined as a result of weakness in the restaurant industry.&#160; Globally, sales volume was also affected by
an ongoing strategy to reduce low margin business, which reduced Company sales
1% in 2007.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Following a 1.0
percentage point increase in 2006, gross profit margin declined 0.1 percentage
points in 2007.&#160; On a comparable basis,
excluding the impact of restructuring charges, gross profit margin declined 0.5
percentage points in 2007.&#160; While the
Company realized incremental cost reductions from its restructuring program,
these savings along with pricing actions did not fully offset the gross profit
margin impact of higher raw material costs.&#160;
As a percentage of net sales, selling, general and administrative
expenses were 27.7% in 2007 compared to 28.4% in 2006.&#160; This reduction was mainly due to cost savings
related to the Company&#146;s restructuring program.&#160;
This benefit was a primary factor in increased operating income margin
which rose 2.2 percentage points in 2007.&#160;
Excluding the impact of restructuring charges, operating income margin
increased 0.3 percentage points.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Earnings per share in
2007 were $1.73 compared to $1.50 in 2006.&#160;
Activities related to the Company&#146;s restructuring program reduced
earnings per share in 2007 and 2006.&#160;
Excluding the impact of these restructuring activities, earnings per
share rose 12% or $0.20 from 2006.&#160;
Higher sales and operating income margin added $0.18 to earnings per
share.&#160; Earnings per share were further
increased by income from unconsolidated operations and minority interest which
added $0.03, and a 2% reduction in diluted shares outstanding which added
$0.03.&#160; The net impact of higher interest
expense and interest income lowered earnings per share by $0.03, with a further
reduction of $0.01 primarily from the tax rate in 2007 versus 2006.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During 2007, the Company
used cash from operations and increased debt to fund $157 million of share repurchases, $104 million of dividend payments and $77
million of net capital expenditures.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Fourth quarter results</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the fourth quarter of
2007, the Company increased sales 7% over the comparable period of 2006.&#160; In local currency the increase was 3%, which
was due to pricing actions and favorable product mix.&#160; While volume gains in international markets
were particularly strong, early shipments of U.S. holiday products in the third
quarter of 2007 reduced sales in the fourth quarter of 2007 by an estimated
1%.&#160; Volume was also affected by the
impact of restaurant industry weakness on the U.S. industrial business.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In the fourth quarter,
the Company continued to be impacted by higher commodity costs which were only
partially offset by cost reductions and pricing actions.&#160; Gross profit margin in the fourth quarter of
2007 was 43.2% compared to 44.3% in the prior year, a decline of 1.1 percentage
points.&#160; On a comparable basis, excluding
the impact of restructuring charges, gross profit margin declined 1.7
percentage points in the fourth quarter.&#160;
Toward the end of fiscal year 2007 and in early fiscal year 2008,
pricing actions were taken and are underway in both the consumer and industrial
businesses to offset increased commodity costs, a rise in packaging costs and
higher energy costs.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\c900132\08-3484-1\task2631690\3484-1-mm.htm',USER='c900132',CD='Jan 23 16:29 2008' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Fourth quarter earnings
per share were $0.67 compared to $0.62 in the fourth quarter of 2006.&#160; Activities related to the Company&#146;s
restructuring program reduced earnings per share in the fourth quarter of 2007
and 2006.&#160; Excluding this impact, the
increase over the fourth quarter of 2006 was $0.03.&#160; During the quarter higher sales and cost
reductions, net of unfavorable raw material costs contributed $0.01 to earnings
per share.&#160; Increased income from
unconsolidated operations and lower shares outstanding each added another
$0.02, offset by unfavorable impacts of $0.01 from a higher tax rate and $0.01
from increased interest expense.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Financial outlook</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Mr.&nbsp;Wilson
continued, &#147;Looking ahead to 2008, we expect another year of solid sales and
profit growth.&#160; Our new product line-up
includes innovative products like flavored pepper and &#147;Crusting Blends&#148; in the
U.S. and in Europe, the expansion of our successful &#147;Toppers&#148; range into
additional markets as well as the introduction of premium products in new
packaging formats.&#160; For industrial
customers we are working on a number of new products with particular interest in
products that promote health and wellness.&#160;
We continue to revitalize our core brands in key markets with new
merchandising systems and more effective marketing.&#160; In the U.S. we have reset over 8,500 stores
with new gravity-fed, easier to shop merchandising systems, and expect to reach
our goal of 12,000 to14,000 stores by the end of
2008.&#160; Acquisitions are a key component
of our growth strategy and the agreement to acquire Lawry&#146;s, which is currently
undergoing regulatory approval, is the latest example of progress with this
strategy.&#160; At this point, we have moved
to the second request phase of the regulatory review process and we are
continuing to work diligently with the regulatory agency to obtain clearance.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;In
2008, the last year of our restructuring program, we expect to achieve up to
$10 million of additional cost reductions.&#160;
We are pursuing a number of supply chain initiatives to realize further
expense savings as well as reductions in inventory.&#160; These savings, along with price increases in
both our consumer and industrial business and a favorable business mix, should
help offset the anticipated unfavorable impact of raw material, packaging
material and energy increases in 2008.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On
a comparable basis, excluding restructuring activities, the Company expects to
increase 2008 earnings per share 8 to 10%.&#160;
Sales are expected to grow 4 to 6% with new product introductions,
revitalization of core brands, price increases and in the first part of 2008, favorable foreign exchange rates.&#160; This sales goal is net of reductions from the
elimination of lower margin products, which is part of the Company&#146;s
restructuring program.&#160; The Company
projects a gross profit margin increase of approximately 0.25 percentage points
on a comparable basis with 2007, excluding restructuring charges.&#160; Including estimated restructuring charges of
$0.10, earnings per share for 2008 are projected to be in the range of $1.97 to
$2.01.&#160; The impact of the Lawry&#146;s
acquisition will not be included in the Company&#146;s projections until the
transaction is completed.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Business
Segment Results</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For fiscal year 2007, the
Company grew consumer business sales 7% compared to 2006, with an increase of
4% in local currency.&#160; The increase was
driven by favorable pricing and product mix, the acquisition of Simply Asia
Foods and volume from brand revitalization, effective marketing programs and
new products.&#160; Consumer sales in the
Americas rose 6% from 2006.&#160; Together,
favorable foreign exchange rates and incremental sales from Simply Asia Foods
added 3% to sales.&#160; Pricing on certain
items such as pepper and favorable product mix further increased sales.&#160; Higher volumes of Hispanic items, the
expanded organic line, grinders and seafood items were offset by lower volumes
on other items including pepper and warehouse club products.&#160; In Europe, consumer sales rose 11% from 2006,
or 2% in local currency, due primarily to pricing actions and volume increases
in the U.K. and France.&#160; During the first
three quarters of 2007, sales growth was offset in part by the impact of a
competitive situation in The Netherlands and the Company&#146;s action to close its
business in Finland which both occurred in 2006.&#160; In the Asia/Pacific region, the Company
increased consumer sales 12%, and in local currency, 4%.&#160; Sales in China rose 20% in local currency
offset by lower sales performance in Australia.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the consumer
business, 2007 operating income, excluding restructuring charges, was $314
million compared to $278 million in 2006.&#160;
Operating income margin rose to 18.8% from 17.9% in 2006 as a result of
cost savings from the Company&#146;s restructuring program and a more favorable
business mix, especially in Europe.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the fourth quarter,
the Company grew consumer sales 6% compared to the prior year, and in local
currency, the increase was 3%.&#160; The early
shipment of U.S. holiday products in the third quarter reduced fourth quarter
sales by 2%.&#160; Sales in the Americas rose
2% from 2006, or 1% in local currency, due primarily to increased
pricing and favorable product mix.&#160; The
impact of the earlier shipments reduced fourth quarter sales volume in this
region by 3%.&#160; During the quarter,
increased volume of Hispanic items and the organic line of products were offset
by lower volumes of pepper and warehouse club products, and the elimination of
several underperforming items.&#160; Consumer
sales in Europe rose 19%, or 8% in local currency,
versus 2006 with increases in its two largest markets, the U.K. and
France.&#160; In the Asia/Pacific region, the
Company increased consumer sales 16%, and in local currency the increase was
3%.&#160; Consumer business operating income
in the fourth quarter of 2007, excluding restructuring charges, rose to $130
million from $122 million in 2006.&#160; This
increase was at the same pace as the increase in fourth quarter sales.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For fiscal year 2007, the
Company grew sales of the industrial business 7% compared to the prior year,
with a 5% increase in local currency.&#160;
The increase was driven primarily by higher pricing to reflect the
increased costs of pepper as well as certain commodities including cheese,
soybean oil and flour.&#160; The elimination
of low margin business reduced 2007 sales by 2%.&#160; In the Americas, industrial sales rose 2%,
from 2006, or 1% in local currency.&#160; The
elimination of low margin business in this region also reduced sales 2%.&#160; An increase of 3% was primarily due to price
increases.&#160; During 2007, new products and
other sales gains with food manufacturers</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\c900132\08-3484-1\task2631690\3484-1-mm.htm',USER='c900132',CD='Jan 23 16:29 2008' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">were</font>
offset by weakness in the restaurant industry.&#160;
In Europe, the Company increased industrial sales 20% from 2006, or 11%
in local currency, with increases in snack seasonings and products sold to
quick service restaurants.&#160; The
elimination of low margin business reduced sales by 2% during the year.&#160; Sales in the Asia/Pacific region increased 26%, or 18% in local currency, led by rapid expansion of
industrial business, especially in China.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the industrial
business, fiscal year 2007 operating income, excluding restructuring charges,
was $74 million compared to $76 million in 2006.&#160; Although the Company realized cost savings
from its restructuring program in 2007, higher commodity costs had a
significant impact.&#160; Toward the end of
2007, pricing actions had been implemented to offset much of the cost increase.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the fourth quarter,
similar factors affected industrial sales in each region.&#160; In total, the Company grew industrial sales
8% compared to the fourth quarter of 2006, and in local currency the increase
was 4%.&#160; The elimination of low margin
business reduced sales 1% during this period.&#160;
Sales in the Americas rose 3%, or 2% in local
currency, from the comparable period for the prior year.&#160; During the fourth quarter, the elimination of
low margin business reduced sales 1% in this region.&#160; Industrial sales in Europe rose 20% from the
fourth quarter of 2006, and in local currency the increase was 11%.&#160; The elimination of low margin business
reduced sales in this region 1%.&#160; In the
Asia/Pacific region, the Company increased sales 19%,
or 9% in local currency.&#160; Fourth quarter
operating income excluding restructuring charges was $17 million compared to
$23 million in 2006.&#160; During this period,
the benefit of restructuring savings and pricing actions did not keep pace with
a steep increase in commodity costs, resulting in a decline in operating
income.&#160; Toward the end of 2007, pricing
actions had been implemented to offset much of the cost increase.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Non-GAAP
Financial Measures</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
pro forma information excluding restructuring activities in this press release are not measures that are defined in generally accepted
accounting principles (&#147;GAAP&#148;).&#160;
Management believes the pro forma information is important for purposes
of comparison to prior periods and development of future projections and
earnings growth prospects.&#160; This
information is also used by management to measure the profitability of our
on-going operations.&#160; Management analyzes
the Company&#146;s business performance and trends excluding amounts related to the
restructuring.&#160; These measures provide a
more consistent view of performance than the closest GAAP equivalent for
management and investors.&#160; Management
compensates for this by using these measures in combination with the GAAP
measures.&#160; The presentation of the
non-GAAP measures in this press release are made alongside the most directly
comparable GAAP measures.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Pro
forma Information</font></b></p>

below certain pro forma financial results excluding amounts related to a
restructuring program in 2007 and 2006.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">About
McCormick</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">McCormick&nbsp;&amp;
Company, Incorporated is the global leader in the manufacture, marketing and
distribution of spices, seasonings and flavors to the entire food industry &#150; to
foodservice and food manufacturers as well as to retail outlets.</font></p>
